\doxysubsection{详细描述}
\subsubsection*{template$<$typename RCU, typename Key, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, typename Traits$>$\newline
class cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Map$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}
Lock-\/free skip-\/list map (template specialization for \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_desc}{RCU}) 

\label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListMap_rcu}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListMap_rcu}%
 The implementation of well-\/known probabilistic data structure called skip-\/list invented by W.\+Pugh in his papers\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{[}1989\mbox{]} W.\+Pugh Skip Lists\+: \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} Probabilistic Alternative to Balanced Trees
\item \mbox{[}1990\mbox{]} W.\+Pugh \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} Skip \doxylink{class_list}{List} Cookbook
\end{DoxyItemize}

\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} skip-\/list is a probabilistic data structure that provides expected logarithmic time search without the need of rebalance. The skip-\/list is a collection of sorted linked list. Nodes are ordered by key. Each node is linked into a subset of the lists. Each list has a level, ranging from 0 to 32. The bottom-\/level list contains all the nodes, and each higher-\/level list is a sublist of the lower-\/level lists. Each node is created with a random top level (with a random height), and belongs to all lists up to that level. The probability that a node has the height 1 is 1/2. The probability that a node has the height N is 1/2 \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} N (more precisely, the distribution depends on an random generator provided, but our generators have this property).

The lock-\/free variant of skip-\/list is implemented according to book
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{[}2008\mbox{]} M.\+Herlihy, N.\+Shavit "{}\+The Art of Multiprocessor Programming"{}, chapter 14.\+4 "{}\+A Lock-\/\+Free Concurrent Skiplist"{}
\end{DoxyItemize}

Template arguments\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily RCU} -\/ one of \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_gc}{RCU type}.
\item {\ttfamily K} -\/ type of a key to be stored in the list.
\item {\ttfamily T} -\/ type of a value to be stored in the list.
\item {\ttfamily Traits} -\/ map traits, default is {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1container_1_1skip__list_1_1traits}{skip\+\_\+list\+::traits}}. It is possible to declare option-\/based list with {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1container_1_1skip__list_1_1make__traits}{cds\+::container\+::skip\+\_\+list\+::make\+\_\+traits}} metafunction instead of {\ttfamily Traits} template argument.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Like STL map class, {\ttfamily Skip\+List\+Map} stores its key-\/value pair as {\ttfamily std\+:pair$<$ K const, T$>$}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Before including {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\doxylink{skip__list__map__rcu_8h}{cds/container/skip\+\_\+list\+\_\+map\+\_\+rcu.\+h}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} you should include appropriate RCU header file, see \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_gc}{RCU type} for list of existing RCU class and corresponding header files.
\end{DoxyNote}
{\bfseries{Iterators}}

The class supports a forward iterator (\doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ae8de0e2b1f72007dd753bbf7191a8523}{iterator} and \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ad2ce464e550466bf72dd0f387cf71d3c}{const\+\_\+iterator}). The iteration is ordered. You may iterate over skip-\/list set items only under RCU lock. Only in this case the iterator is thread-\/safe since while RCU is locked any set\textquotesingle{}s item cannot be reclaimed.

The requirement of RCU lock during iterating means that deletion of the elements (i.\+e. \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a33830c59e1a27dc4f04c106ba7f148d6}{erase}) is not possible.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
The iterator object cannot be passed between threads
\end{DoxyWarning}
The iterator class supports the following minimalistic interface\+:

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{iterator}{iterator}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_a457e4cc42df8bd25208a4a2e0dc80b2e} 
typedef skip\+\_\+list\+::details\+::iterator$<$ typename base\+\_\+class\+::iterator $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::iterator}



Iterator type 

The forward iterator has some features\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item it is ordered
\item it has no post-\/increment operator
\item to protect the value, the iterator contains a GC-\/specific guard + another guard is required locally for increment operator. For some GC (like as {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1gc_af0523881f089593a7559d194ee2b5dd9}{gc\+::\+HP}}), a guard is a limited resource per thread, so an exception (or assertion) "{}no free guard"{} may be thrown if the limit of guard count per thread is exceeded.
\item The iterator cannot be moved across thread boundary because it contains thread-\/private GC\textquotesingle{}s guard.
\item Iterator ensures thread-\/safety even if you delete the item the iterator points to. However, in case of concurrent deleting operations there is no guarantee that you iterate all item in the list. Moreover, a crash is possible when you try to iterate the next element that has been deleted by concurrent thread.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
Use this iterator on the concurrent container for debugging purpose only.
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
{\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a0e2c4d5bc6c6536740cea06b2d8110a9}{end()}} and {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a9152b392635f558460606be3facbb686}{cend()}} are not dereferenceable.
\end{DoxyNote}

typedef skip\+\_\+list\+::details\+::iterator$<$ typename base\+\_\+class\+::iterator $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::iterator}



Forward iterator 

The forward iterator has some features\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item it has no post-\/increment operator
\item it depends on iterator of underlying {\ttfamily Ordered\+List} 
\end{DoxyItemize}

You may safely use iterators in multi-\/threaded environment only under RCU lock. Otherwise, a crash is possible if another thread deletes the element the iterator points to. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_a8dbded437267b9bcf6d49660d240a956}\index{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!key\_comparator@{key\_comparator}}

Checks whether the map contains {\ttfamily key} 

The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and returns {\ttfamily true} if it is found, and {\ttfamily false} otherwise.

Checks whether the set contains {\ttfamily key} using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is similar to {\ttfamily contains( key )} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily Less} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_aa974b413e15121f36efe968d90ab758e}\index{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!contains@{contains}}

 The function searches an item with key {\ttfamily key}, calls {\ttfamily f} functor and deletes the item. If {\ttfamily key} is not found, the functor is not called.

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::erase\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{K const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Deletes the item from the map using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListMap_erase_val}{erase(K const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily Less} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the map. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ae8ecd16cab44082e831187b7fbd5add2}\index{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!erase\_with@{erase\_with}}
\index{erase\_with@{erase\_with}!cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{erase\_with()}{erase\_with()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ae8ecd16cab44082e831187b7fbd5add2} 
template$<$typename RCU, typename Key, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, typename Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename K, typename Less$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::erase\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{K const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Deletes the item from the map using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListMap_rcu_erase_val}{erase(K const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily Less} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the map. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_a13609ab5691e882619a6bbf43f4d9619}\index{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!erase\_with@{erase\_with}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{extract()}{extract()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_a7784b99ef7041b7083ed978b854f002d} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_ad354cc5fb06255b8d60c87c2a20ebedc}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{K const \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts the item from the map with specified {\ttfamily key} 

\label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListMap_hp_extract}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListMap_hp_extract}%
The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} in the map, unlinks it from the map, and returns a guarded pointer to the item found. If {\ttfamily key} is not found the function returns an empty guarded pointer.

Note the compare functor should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily K} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a990b253457b725e094c126ea9a71fef3}{key\+\_\+type}}.

The item extracted is freed automatically by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} when returned {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_ad354cc5fb06255b8d60c87c2a20ebedc}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object will be destroyed or released. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_ad354cc5fb06255b8d60c87c2a20ebedc}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses the GC\textquotesingle{}s guard that can be limited resource.
\end{DoxyNote}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ad793833cd6a6363a487427e4ee31d531}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{K const \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts the item from the map with specified {\ttfamily key} 

\label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListMap_rcu_extract}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListMap_rcu_extract}%
The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} in the map, unlinks it from the set, and returns \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1exempt__ptr}{exempt\+\_\+ptr} pointer to the item found. If the item is not found the function returns an empty {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ad793833cd6a6363a487427e4ee31d531}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}} 

Note the compare functor from {\ttfamily Traits} class\textquotesingle{} template argument should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily K} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a990b253457b725e094c126ea9a71fef3}{key\+\_\+type}}.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize()} method can be called. RCU should NOT be locked.

The function does not free the item found. The item will be implicitly freed when the returned object is destroyed or when its {\ttfamily release()} member function is called. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_af7dee701d905f4f39facecc4d476720d}\index{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!extract\_max@{extract\_max}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{extract\_max()}{extract\_max()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}

Extracts an item with maximal key from the map 

The function searches an item with maximal key, unlinks it, and returns a guarded pointer to item found. If the skip-\/list is empty the function returns an empty {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_ad354cc5fb06255b8d60c87c2a20ebedc}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}}.

The item found is freed by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} automatically when returned {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_ad354cc5fb06255b8d60c87c2a20ebedc}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object will be destroyed or released. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_ad354cc5fb06255b8d60c87c2a20ebedc}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses the GC\textquotesingle{}s guard that can be limited resource.
\end{DoxyNote}

Extracts an item with maximal key from the map 

The function searches an item with maximal key, unlinks it from the set, and returns \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1exempt__ptr}{exempt\+\_\+ptr} pointer to the item. If the skip-\/list is empty the function returns an empty {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ad793833cd6a6363a487427e4ee31d531}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}}.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should NOT be locked.

The function does not free the item found. The item will be implicitly freed when the returned object is destroyed or when its {\ttfamily release()} member function is called. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_a21c2f86a5ac435b83b99d39805790332}\index{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!extract\_min@{extract\_min}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_ad354cc5fb06255b8d60c87c2a20ebedc}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract\+\_\+min (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts an item with minimal key from the map 

The function searches an item with minimal key, unlinks it, and returns an guarded pointer to the item found. If the skip-\/list is empty the function returns an empty guarded pointer.

The item extracted is freed automatically by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} when returned {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_ad354cc5fb06255b8d60c87c2a20ebedc}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object will be destroyed or released. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_ad354cc5fb06255b8d60c87c2a20ebedc}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses the GC\textquotesingle{}s guard that can be limited resource.
\end{DoxyNote}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ad793833cd6a6363a487427e4ee31d531}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract\+\_\+min (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts an item with minimal key from the map 

The function searches an item with minimal key, unlinks it, and returns \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1exempt__ptr}{exempt\+\_\+ptr} pointer to the item. If the skip-\/list is empty the function returns an empty {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ad793833cd6a6363a487427e4ee31d531}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}}.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should NOT be locked.

The function does not free the item found. The item will be implicitly freed when the returned object is destroyed or when its {\ttfamily release()} member function is called. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_a497e3d92841382816e09b48a243a4e85}\index{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!extract\_with@{extract\_with}}
\index{extract\_with@{extract\_with}!cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{extract\_with()}{extract\_with()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_a497e3d92841382816e09b48a243a4e85} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_ad354cc5fb06255b8d60c87c2a20ebedc}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{K const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts the item from the map with comparing functor {\ttfamily pred} 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListMap_hp_extract}{extract(K const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} predicate is used for key comparing.

{\ttfamily Less} functor has the semantics like {\ttfamily std\+::less} but should take arguments of type \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a990b253457b725e094c126ea9a71fef3}{key\+\_\+type} and {\ttfamily K} in any order. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the map. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_af5ebe0f106a85072767a297ae4ecbb36}\index{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!extract\_with@{extract\_with}}
\index{extract\_with@{extract\_with}!cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{extract\_with()}{extract\_with()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_af5ebe0f106a85072767a297ae4ecbb36} 
template$<$typename RCU, typename Key, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, typename Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename K, typename Less$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ad793833cd6a6363a487427e4ee31d531}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{K const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

The function is an analog of {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_affbd6d8a9164159c2813ea4c33ce3172}{extract(\+K const\&)}} but {\ttfamily pred} predicate is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} has the semantics like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the map. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_ad04df5f693d7581836b929d89290dee6}\index{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!find@{find}}

Finds the key {\ttfamily val} using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListMap_find_cfunc}{find(K const\&, Func)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily Less} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the map. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_aa0eb86986df2465845d0bc922a762ebf}\index{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!find\_with@{find\_with}}

Finds the key {\ttfamily val} using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListMap_rcu_find_cfunc}{find(K const\&, Func)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily Less} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the map. 函数调用图\+:
% FIG 7
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_a123229b5e06a28eff5eb29b2609594ec}\index{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!get@{get}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{get()}{get()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_a123229b5e06a28eff5eb29b2609594ec} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_ad354cc5fb06255b8d60c87c2a20ebedc}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{structget}{\+::get}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{K const \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds the key {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

\label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListMap_hp_get}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListMap_hp_get}%
The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and returns a guarded pointer to the item found. If {\ttfamily key} is not found the function returns an empty guarded pointer.

It is safe when a concurrent thread erases the item returned as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_ad354cc5fb06255b8d60c87c2a20ebedc}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}}. In this case the item will be freed later by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} automatically when {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_ad354cc5fb06255b8d60c87c2a20ebedc}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object will be destroyed or released. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_ad354cc5fb06255b8d60c87c2a20ebedc}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses one GC\textquotesingle{}s guard which can be limited resource.
\end{DoxyNote}

Note the compare functor specified for class {\ttfamily Traits} template parameter should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily K} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a36b61c74c698c225b2835c56f6d15376}{value\+\_\+type}}. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a4f720be58b42f25432176750a6534029}\index{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!get@{get}}

Finds the key {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

\label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListMap_rcu_get}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListMap_rcu_get}%
The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and returns a {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a8af29d35cb5176743c6ad76fab351ccd}{raw\+\_\+ptr}} object pointing to an item found. If {\ttfamily key} is not found it returns empty {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a8af29d35cb5176743c6ad76fab351ccd}{raw\+\_\+ptr}}.

Note the compare functor in {\ttfamily Traits} class\textquotesingle{} template argument should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily K} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a990b253457b725e094c126ea9a71fef3}{key\+\_\+type}}.

RCU should be locked before call of this function. Returned item is valid only while RCU is locked\+:

Finds the key {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListMap_hp_get}{get( K const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for comparing the keys.

{\ttfamily Less} functor has the semantics like {\ttfamily std\+::less} but should take arguments of type \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a990b253457b725e094c126ea9a71fef3}{key\+\_\+type} and {\ttfamily K} in any order. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the map. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a8ee63cb325e31fa057c2c4334500c8e8}\index{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!get\_with@{get\_with}}

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SkipListMap_rcu_get}{get(K const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for comparing the keys.

Inserts new node with key and default value 

The function creates a node with {\ttfamily key} and default value, and then inserts the node created into the map.

Preconditions\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a990b253457b725e094c126ea9a71fef3}{key\+\_\+type}} should be constructible from a value of type {\ttfamily K}. In trivial case, {\ttfamily K} is equal to {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a990b253457b725e094c126ea9a71fef3}{key\+\_\+type}}.
\item The {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ae78036d3bb19ae9dc00d148a03fc7fd2}{mapped\+\_\+type}} should be default-\/constructible.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a990b253457b725e094c126ea9a71fef3}{key\+\_\+type}} should be constructible from {\ttfamily key} of type {\ttfamily K}.

\end{DoxyItemize}

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should not be locked.

Returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily val} is inserted into the set, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_aaf451841ee82289c5a442c619346d02b}\index{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!insert\_with@{insert\_with}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_aaf451841ee82289c5a442c619346d02b}

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::insert\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const K \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Func}]{func}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Inserts new node and initialize it by a functor 

This function inserts new node with key {\ttfamily key} and if inserting is successful then it calls {\ttfamily func} functor with signature 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{operator()}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{item}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}


The argument {\ttfamily item} of user-\/defined functor {\ttfamily func} is the reference to the map\textquotesingle{}s item inserted\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily item.\+first} is a const reference to item\textquotesingle{}s key that cannot be changed.
\item {\ttfamily item.\+second} is a reference to item\textquotesingle{}s value that may be changed.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The function allows to split creating of new item into three part\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item create item from {\ttfamily key};
\item insert new item into the map;
\item if inserting is successful, initialize the value of item by calling {\ttfamily func} functor
\end{DoxyItemize}

This can be useful if complete initialization of object of {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a36b61c74c698c225b2835c56f6d15376}{value\+\_\+type}} is heavyweight and it is preferable that the initialization should be completed only if inserting is successful.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should not be locked. 函数调用图\+:
% FIG 9
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_a3c1d51549a3942e8d75f8361adf6ce9e}\index{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SkipListMap$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!insert\_with@{insert\_with}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{insert\_with()}{insert\_with()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_a14e0bb6b5343b4cf694b8da93c8f4a03} 
std\+::pair$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{K const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Func}]{func}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}}]{b\+Insert}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a41f9c5fb8b08eb5dc3edce4dcb37fee7}{true}}}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Updates data by {\ttfamily key} 

The operation performs inserting or changing data with lock-\/free manner.

If the {\ttfamily key} not found in the map, then the new item created from {\ttfamily key} will be inserted into the map iff {\ttfamily b\+Insert} is {\ttfamily true} (note that in this case the \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a990b253457b725e094c126ea9a71fef3}{key\+\_\+type} should be constructible from type {\ttfamily K}). Otherwise, if {\ttfamily key} is found, the functor {\ttfamily func} is called with item found. The functor {\ttfamily Func} signature\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{my\_functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{operator()}}(\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{bNew}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{item}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily b\+New} -\/ {\ttfamily true} if the item has been inserted, {\ttfamily false} otherwise
\item {\ttfamily item} -\/ item of the map
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor may change any fields of the {\ttfamily item.\+second} that is \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a36b61c74c698c225b2835c56f6d15376}{value\+\_\+type}.

Returns {\ttfamily  std\+::pair$<$bool, bool$>$ } where {\ttfamily first} is {\ttfamily true} if operation is successful, {\ttfamily second} is {\ttfamily true} if new item has been added or {\ttfamily false} if {\ttfamily key} already exists.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
See \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1intrusive_cds_intrusive_item_creating}{insert item troubleshooting} 
\end{DoxyWarning}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a733cd6a7899602cbe2667ddf1764ea5b}

template$<$typename K, typename Func$>$ \\
std\+::pair$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{cds\+::container\+::\+Skip\+List\+Map}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{K const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Func}]{func}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}}]{b\+Insert}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a41f9c5fb8b08eb5dc3edce4dcb37fee7}{true}}}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Updates data by {\ttfamily key} 

The operation performs inserting or changing data with lock-\/free manner.

If the {\ttfamily key} not found in the map, then the new item created from {\ttfamily key} is inserted into the map iff {\ttfamily b\+Insert} is {\ttfamily true}. Otherwise, if {\ttfamily key} found, the functor {\ttfamily func} is called with item found. The functor {\ttfamily Func} interface is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{my\_functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{operator()}}(\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{bNew}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_skip_list_map}{item}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily b\+New} -\/ {\ttfamily true} if the item has been inserted, {\ttfamily false} otherwise
\item {\ttfamily item} -\/ item of the map
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor may change any fields of {\ttfamily item.\+second}.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize()} method can be called. RCU should not be locked.

Returns {\ttfamily  std\+::pair$<$bool, bool$>$ } where {\ttfamily first} is {\ttfamily true} if operation is successful, {\ttfamily second} is {\ttfamily true} if new item has been added or {\ttfamily false} if the item with {\ttfamily key} already exists.
